comment48:I do not strongly support Donald Trump, nor do I strongly support Hillary Clinton. What I do strongly support, however, is respect for my fellow citizens regardless of their political ideologies. Categorizing republicans as "uneducated" and "racist white males" only promotes hatred and division in our nation. If you are a minority (by race, gender, sexual orientation, etc.), then how can you expect equality and social justice if you don't reciprocate it? Calling people "bigoted" solely based on their political beliefs will not change who is president. Endless arguing on social media will only divide us further, fueling hatred amongst citizens of the same nation.

Regardless of who is president, it is important to respect the views of others. Don't let the election control your anger. The president is only the president. WE are the citizens and WE are the ones who build our nation. WE are the intellectuals that fuel innovation, WE are the workers that builds the foundations on which America lays. There are more of US than there are of them. The people do not represent the government, they represent US.

Our nation can only progress if we work together. Look past each others political beliefs, listen to each others ideas, and learn from each other. Only when we are willing to listen to each other can we build together.

Love each other and stand unified, then we can succeed.
